<span id="freeTextContainer9793908109336033248">Every time someone out there buys a Mike Gayle book, another little bit of me dies.<br /><br />You know I feel far, far more satisfaction in writing about books I thought were awful that were good. And tonight I remembered that woeful book by Mike Gayle 'My Legendary Girlfriend'. Also this is to warn others. It's so bad you will want to pan fry your eyes in garlic butter and feed them to Michael Winner.<br /><br />I think that's a very important to know the risks when reading this sort of bile. People need to be protec</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText9793908109336033248">Every time someone out there buys a Mike Gayle book, another little bit of me dies.<br /><br />You know I feel far, far more satisfaction in writing about books I thought were awful that were good. And tonight I remembered that woeful book by Mike Gayle 'My Legendary Girlfriend'. Also this is to warn others. It's so bad you will want to pan fry your eyes in garlic butter and feed them to Michael Winner.<br /><br />I think that's a very important to know the risks when reading this sort of bile. People need to be protected from it, in the same way that no one protected me, namely Robin as it was his book. Why didn't you protect me from this book. Why Robin, why? <br /><br /><em>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_124359501">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/124359501" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/4149886-mags" class="left imgcol" title="Mags"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1424062482p2/4149886.jpg" alt="Mags" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/124359501?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Oct 02, 2010</a>

      <a href="/user/show/4149886-mags" class="user" title="Mags">Mags</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/828402.My_Legendary_Girlfriend" title="Paperback 9780340718162" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">People who just came from a break-up and needs some promise and sympathy</span></div>

        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a onclick="Effect.toggle('reviewTextContainer124359501'); return false;" href="#">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span style="display:none" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer124359501">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11058125565934693429">This book, it depressed me. It felt like I was being dragged through a very slow and painful death--Will Kelley's death. This novel is like a rubber band that's stretched too far and would most likely snap. Which would make it deserve at least 3 stars, but I gave it a 4 because I liked how I didn't expect the ending. I'm GLAD he got up, move on, and never returned to that Agnes girl who's probably going to end up with an idiot. Will is a lovable character, and my pity and sympathy were turned to</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText11058125565934693429">This book, it depressed me. It felt like I was being dragged through a very slow and painful death--Will Kelley's death. This novel is like a rubber band that's stretched too far and would most likely snap. Which would make it deserve at least 3 stars, but I gave it a 4 because I liked how I didn't expect the ending. I'm GLAD he got up, move on, and never returned to that Agnes girl who's probably going to end up with an idiot. Will is a lovable character, and my pity and sympathy were turned to him during the time I was reading his enlongated stories as his days of depression pass by.<br /><br />I also love Mike Gayle's narration, and how there's a twist in every corner. There will be times that the story is boring--be warned. It made me think, "When will all this whining over a girl who doesn't deserve his 'great love' ever end?" But I don't want to go into the advice of "Move the fuck on and stop being a pussy" because we've all been through this not-over-it-yet phase. And Gayle sure has been through a LOT of real-life heartbreak stories (he's a relationship adviser of some sort), so he surely knows what he's talking about.<br /><br />So, anyway, 4 stars, because I like Gayle for his realistic writing, and I love his website for advices for first-time writers.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="11058125565934693429">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a href="/review/show/90264655?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Apr 12, 2010</a>

      <a href="/user/show/1099897-brian" class="user" title="Brian">Brian</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="did not like it">did not like it</span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/442087.My_Legendary_Girlfriend" title="Paperback 9780767906555" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer90264655">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8959971643811009862"> Okay, I wanted to not really say anything about this book since I thought it was so horrible and I don't really like to say anything too pessimistic...but this novel bugged me so much that after all this time I just felt compelled to write about it. <br /> I was kind of going through a slump of bad books lately. Not horrible, just not finding anything entertaining and feeling like I was kind of slogging through the thing just to finish it. But My Legendary Girlfriend tops them all off! <br /> The writing w</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText8959971643811009862"> Okay, I wanted to not really say anything about this book since I thought it was so horrible and I don't really like to say anything too pessimistic...but this novel bugged me so much that after all this time I just felt compelled to write about it. <br /> I was kind of going through a slump of bad books lately. Not horrible, just not finding anything entertaining and feeling like I was kind of slogging through the thing just to finish it. But My Legendary Girlfriend tops them all off! <br /> The writing was horrible and the characters were totally annoying. I hated the fact that it was written from a first person perspective because the main character was so pathetic and I had no interest in knowing what he was thinking or the reasoning of his actions. If there were examples of why this ex-girlfriend of his was so legendary I could maybe see the point but there's no reference to their past relationship that would warrant him missing her so much. What few things he does cite just make her seem totally evil. <br /> So I don't know if it's just because I don't understand British humor (which I will admit I am not a big fan of) or if the writing and story is just as bad as I think it is. I just know from my perspective that it was a really tough novel for me to get through and it was getting me to the point of frustration. I've never started a novel that I didn't complete but this is quite possibly the only one I was very, very close to not finishing.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="8959971643811009862">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer194762865">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8086464809543727205">I never would have found Mike Gayle had it not been for my flatmate insisting I read one of his books. I have to admit I wasn't too sure at first. The blurb read a bit too much like chick lit novel for my liking. I'm a man, and I like manly things dammit! Luckily I got past my silly male ego and embraced my metrosexuality, and a good few years later and I'm one of Mike Gayle's biggest fans. My Legendary Girlfriend was Gayle's first novel, having spent time as a journalist and features writer. Th</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText8086464809543727205">I never would have found Mike Gayle had it not been for my flatmate insisting I read one of his books. I have to admit I wasn't too sure at first. The blurb read a bit too much like chick lit novel for my liking. I'm a man, and I like manly things dammit! Luckily I got past my silly male ego and embraced my metrosexuality, and a good few years later and I'm one of Mike Gayle's biggest fans. My Legendary Girlfriend was Gayle's first novel, having spent time as a journalist and features writer. This book was a huge success as Gayle followed in the footsteps of fellow lad lit author Nick Hornby to write a book about relationships from a male perspective with very high praise indeed.<br /><br />To read the rest of my review please visit my blog: <br /><a rel="nofollow" href="http://stevenscaffardi.blogspot.co.uk/2012/03/steves-book-reviews-my-legendary.html" target="_blank">http://stevenscaffardi.blogspot.co.uk...</a></span>

      <a href="/user/show/5921785-juliana-graham" class="user" title="Juliana Graham">Juliana Graham</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer277378536">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14243349021710436682">A strange one this. I've had this book on my bookcase since around 2004 when it first came out. I read it then and I LOVED it. It was one of my favourite books EVER. I used to recommend it to people, lend it to people and generally sing its praises.<br /><br />Maybe I identified with the 20 something lead character who was a fairly mediocre teacher wishing to be something else, pining over the love of his life who had cruelly dumped him and generally muddling along waiting for something exciting to happen.</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText14243349021710436682">A strange one this. I've had this book on my bookcase since around 2004 when it first came out. I read it then and I LOVED it. It was one of my favourite books EVER. I used to recommend it to people, lend it to people and generally sing its praises.<br /><br />Maybe I identified with the 20 something lead character who was a fairly mediocre teacher wishing to be something else, pining over the love of his life who had cruelly dumped him and generally muddling along waiting for something exciting to happen. <br /><br />The time came last month for me to re-read the book - I've run out of bookcase and couldn't bear to throw this one out without reading it again and maybe even deciding to keep it if I still loved it as much as I did the first time. I'm sad to say, I didn't. Don't get me wrong, I still enjoyed the book, I still found the occasional part laugh out loud funny, I was still rooting for Will to sort his life out. But there was something missing. Maybe I'm too old and cynical now. Maybe the ever so slightly predictable ending irked me because in real life, things like that don't ever seem to happen. Maybe you should read the book and decide for yourself.<br /><br />My copy has now gone to the charity shop - maybe you'll love it, maybe you'll only like it - but either way it's worth a read and Mike Gayle is great! Still plenty more of his to read...</span>

              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer710746447">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14034604020340428644">I've mostly stopped reading chick lit books because I'm about 10 years out of their demographic range and the older I get, the more immature and whiny the protagonists seem. That said, this looked promising, so I gave it a go. While Will is every bit the whiny, melodramatic 20-something you'd expect, he also has enough heart and charm to win you over. Who hasn't spent too long agonizing over a lost love? Or rushed into a new love too quickly? I'm pleased the author took the time to wrap up every</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText14034604020340428644">I've mostly stopped reading chick lit books because I'm about 10 years out of their demographic range and the older I get, the more immature and whiny the protagonists seem. That said, this looked promising, so I gave it a go. While Will is every bit the whiny, melodramatic 20-something you'd expect, he also has enough heart and charm to win you over. Who hasn't spent too long agonizing over a lost love? Or rushed into a new love too quickly? I'm pleased the author took the time to wrap up everyone's storylines, so nothing was left hanging. The twists were fun and mostly unexpected. This was a fun book to spend a rainy weekend reading. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer64960860">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12544815738008825922">I chose this book from<br /> the relays based on its<br /> pretty cover. Here's a<br /> good piece of advice:<br /> Never judge a book by its<br /> cover...bad or good. That's<br /> all this book had---a cute<br /> cover. I was hopeful that <br /> this book, with its male<br /> protagonist, a first for me<br /> in chick lit, would be clever<br /> and new. Nope. Disappointing<br /> waste of good reading time.<br /></span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_1428952717">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1428952717" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/10323950-best-crime-books-more" class="left imgcol" title="Best Crime Books &amp; More"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1433946891p2/10323950.jpg" alt="Best Crime Books &amp; More" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/1428952717?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Oct 30, 2015</a>

      <a href="/user/show/10323950-best-crime-books-more" class="user" title="Best Crime Books &amp; More">Best Crime Books &amp; More</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok">it was ok</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/442087.My_Legendary_Girlfriend" title="Paperback 9780767906555" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1428952717">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8419958590870870391">Okay, my first foray into the world of Lad Lit came only in November 2011 with a <br />self-published book that had me literally crying with laughter. The book was so <br />good that I immediately started looking at other male ‘Lad Lit’ authors and Mike <br />Gayle was one that I had heard of and was incredibly popular.<br /><br />With that in mind I decided to try his debut novel My Legendary Girlfriend that he <br />first published back in 1998. Very early on we are introduced to Will Kelly, the only <br />real ‘character’ so to speak</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText8419958590870870391">Okay, my first foray into the world of Lad Lit came only in November 2011 with a <br />self-published book that had me literally crying with laughter. The book was so <br />good that I immediately started looking at other male ‘Lad Lit’ authors and Mike <br />Gayle was one that I had heard of and was incredibly popular.<br /><br />With that in mind I decided to try his debut novel My Legendary Girlfriend that he <br />first published back in 1998. Very early on we are introduced to Will Kelly, the only <br />real ‘character’ so to speak in the book. We get the lowdown on his truly depressing <br />life, his awful flat and his agony over his ex-girlfriend.<br /><br />Very early on I found myself disliking Will, all he seemed to do was moan about literally very thing, and I had no sympathy for him whatsoever. I figured that this must be the lead up to where the character develops and the reader ends up seeing the turnaround. No such luck for me on that front.<br /><br />The most frustrating thing is that nothing much happens. I get the impression this was meant to be a mans take on the Bridget Jones style kind of diary; however this is the furthest from that example in my opinion. Seeing as I was over halfway through the book and not feeling anything towards the character, I gave the book a break for a day and hoped I would return with a better feeling.<br /><br />Sadly, when I returned and ploughed through (that’s what it felt like), I finished it with an overwhelming feeling of disappointment. The writing was good, and there were certainly moments that made me chuckle, but that alone was not enough for me to actually feel like I enjoyed the book. <br /><br />Overall, I can honestly say that this book was unmemorable at best and boring at worst. The writing and moments of humour are enough for me to try another Mike Gayle, after all as this was his debut novel and he now has a solid fan base I would like to give a newer book a try and hope that maybe it was just this particular book that wasn’t my cup of tea.<br /></span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="8419958590870870391">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13694209600104472202">I found this in the teen room at the library. I'm thinking that it was an accidental purchase, since it's definitely geared to an adult audience, but when you read the blurb on the back it could really go either way. It's just when you get into the story-- ugh. If one of my male friends was behaving the way the main character was, I'd have encouraged him to seek psychiatric help rather than dating/marrying him. Will was not lovable. Will drove me nuts. Ick ick icky.</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1051840916">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8708249087297082645">A superb debut novel with an ending I wanted from the start. My wife is a massive fan of Gayle's work and I thought it about time to give one a shot, but I always start from the beginning when starting a new authors bibliography. I'm glad I did as I thoroughly enjoyed this, from beginning to end. It's well written, beautifully crafted and a superb and fresh concept for a plot. I will certainly be picking up some more from Mike Gayle very soon. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_11677136">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/11677136" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/743909-bridget" class="left imgcol" title="Bridget"><img src="http://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" alt="Bridget" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/11677136?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Jan 04, 2008</a>

      <a href="/user/show/743909-bridget" class="user" title="Bridget">Bridget</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/442087.My_Legendary_Girlfriend" title="Paperback 9780767906555" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer11677136">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4429073460295393648">Anyone who's ever gone through a rough breakup - and let's face it, that's all of us - will find literary comfort food in this book. The story spans the course of a weekend, starting with our hero's crushing breakup with his longtime girlfriend. We're with him through the various stages of angst and wondering, but somehow the read is comforting and even funny. I swallowed this book in one weekend and enjoyed the diversion.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <a href="/user/show/11453596-leila" class="left imgcol" title="Leila"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1451790382p2/11453596.jpg" alt="Leila" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/1081702659?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <a href="/user/show/11453596-leila" class="user" title="Leila">Leila</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok">it was ok</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/442087.My_Legendary_Girlfriend" title="Paperback 9780767906555" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1081702659">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10309275759498573460">I had low expectations of this book to start, and I was coming off an epic fail library batch so I wanted some light, diversionary reading. This fit the bill, but it was pretty silly &amp; inane. There were moments of humor, and I think anyone who has spent time single, in a shitty apartment, unmotivated by ambition of any sort can relate to Will's shenanigans. The plot device(s) were very stupid though, and they could've been much better a la Rainbow Rowell or Graeme Simsion, or JoJo Moyes. I t</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText10309275759498573460">I had low expectations of this book to start, and I was coming off an epic fail library batch so I wanted some light, diversionary reading. This fit the bill, but it was pretty silly &amp; inane. There were moments of humor, and I think anyone who has spent time single, in a shitty apartment, unmotivated by ambition of any sort can relate to Will's shenanigans. The plot device(s) were very stupid though, and they could've been much better a la Rainbow Rowell or Graeme Simsion, or JoJo Moyes. I think most fun I had reading this is the nostalgia I felt for the late 90s, before the internet &amp; mobile technology so thoroughly infiltrated life...that being said, this book comes off very dated.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="10309275759498573460">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span style="display:none" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1444002059">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6495784265224542576">The book captivated me, I gave up the book I was reading for this one that for once I read from cover to cover without interruption. I have to admit, I felt connected to Will's youth and situation, perhaps that's what made it even more appealing to me. But I hated how by the end events were happening so fast and without attention to details it deserved as if Mike Gayle said to himself "lets get over with this alreay".<br /><br />I felt betrayed by the ending especially. Surprised yes but also betrayed, the</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText6495784265224542576">The book captivated me, I gave up the book I was reading for this one that for once I read from cover to cover without interruption. I have to admit, I felt connected to Will's youth and situation, perhaps that's what made it even more appealing to me. But I hated how by the end events were happening so fast and without attention to details it deserved as if Mike Gayle said to himself "lets get over with this alreay".<br /><br />I felt betrayed by the ending especially. Surprised yes but also betrayed, the book was building up to a dramatic ending, an ending i would pretty much appreciate honestly, but then no, happy ending as if I was watching a disney movie.</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_1220812613">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1220812613" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/15225906-sankrutyayan" class="left imgcol" title="Sankrutyayan"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1451714937p2/15225906.jpg" alt="Sankrutyayan" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/1220812613?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Apr 11, 2015</a>

      <a href="/user/show/15225906-sankrutyayan" class="user" title="Sankrutyayan">Sankrutyayan</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/828402.My_Legendary_Girlfriend" title="Paperback 9780340718162" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1220812613">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13397549006637291188">This one is fresh. I have not read a funnier description of a heartbroken bachelor before, maybe I have not read enough, yet this would be funnier I speculate. This actually seemed a generalization of a twenty-something bachelor's life and of all his everyday feats. If I had to quote everything that is funny or interesting or entertaining in this book I have to write the whole book here again. This is more of giggling and tittering type than of laugh-out-loud.<br /><br />This book stuck a chord with me too,</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText13397549006637291188">This one is fresh. I have not read a funnier description of a heartbroken bachelor before, maybe I have not read enough, yet this would be funnier I speculate. This actually seemed a generalization of a twenty-something bachelor's life and of all his everyday feats. If I had to quote everything that is funny or interesting or entertaining in this book I have to write the whole book here again. This is more of giggling and tittering type than of laugh-out-loud.<br /><br />This book stuck a chord with me too, like it did with a lot of sulking men out there. It was a little too whiny but author did not hide it, instead mentioned it himself in various ways. I bought Mr.Commitment before this, but before I could complete it I gave it to my only best friend for safe keeping. By safe keeping, I mean that it would never come back to me again. But it is satisfying to think of it as my small token of gift for her tolerant nature towards my complete lack of knowledge about real world and real people and their nature which alters with each person, situation, and time. <br /><br />What stupid things people do when they are in desperate need of company or a partner or when heart broke. I still could not believe that he pulled this profound yet conflicting story through perfectly with humor and wit. The turn of events in just 3 days is stupendous. It was depressing at first to concur with the decision of Will and Kate about the wedding, but I accepted it easily later when I thought of the theory of wedding and marriage in India. There were a lot of things I related myself to with Will. It is not easy to make yourself acceptable and presentable over the phone while talking to a person you have not met before and come out successful. <br /><br />Most of the things I thought I alone would do when I am living in a room all to myself, were described most accurately by Mike. Maybe everyone is alike and it is just best kept secret that makes us all feel different and unique about ourselves. Everybody has a person in their life whom they put on a pedestal and devote themselves to that one person while brooding about miserable turn of events which caused the separation from that one person they choose to be with under all conditions, gay and grave. But there are only few of them who has got an Alice. What of all of who have not got an Alice. With no rhyme or reason some lives are kicked into an unending well of desolation and dejection. Maybe we should never care for someone more than the magnitude of pain we can endure in their absence. Wow, I just formed sentence that does make no sense but feels profound and deep, at least to me. <br /><br />He left a little clue in the form of changing voice and nature of Alice before the climax was thrown into the face of the reader. I grabbed that clue, but still was dubious as he introduced Aggi again.<br /><br />The ending was exemplary. I love this book.<br /><br /></span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="13397549006637291188">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/20682625-zanriel?shelf=lad-lit" class="actionLinkLite">lad-lit</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/20682625-zanriel?shelf=romance-male-pov" class="actionLinkLite">romance-male-pov</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1071639303">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3969198438069050954">I loved this book. The main character was a wreck, but I could totally relate. I've been in his shoes even though I hope I was never quite so desperate. It had a few cringeworthy moments, and the pace seemed a bit slow at times. But all that was necessary to appreciate the full impact of the final payoff.<br /><br />Very much a slice-of-life type story, this book's 277 pages took place mostly in Will's apartment over the course of three or four days. With flashbacks, long phone conversations, and detailed a</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText3969198438069050954">I loved this book. The main character was a wreck, but I could totally relate. I've been in his shoes even though I hope I was never quite so desperate. It had a few cringeworthy moments, and the pace seemed a bit slow at times. But all that was necessary to appreciate the full impact of the final payoff.<br /><br />Very much a slice-of-life type story, this book's 277 pages took place mostly in Will's apartment over the course of three or four days. With flashbacks, long phone conversations, and detailed accounts of every moment, thought, and feeling Will experienced, the author paints a vivid portrait of a man's life. He's a pathetic, obsessive, lonely, aimless, tortured man, right on the cusp of his 26th birthday. Even so, you want him to be okay, to "get sorted". He's a hopeless romantic, and darnit but doesn't the world need more of those?<br /><br />The story is full of witty lines, touching moments, angst, and cultural references. It's set around the mid 90's so it's nostalgic too.<br /><br />There are overlapping, sometimes imaginary love triangles, longings, regrets, shocking revelations, apathy, and redemption.<br /><br />If you have even a single romantic bone in your body and you're in the mood for a book where the main character is flawed but likeable, you should read this book.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="3969198438069050954">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <a href="/user/show/300958-stephanie" class="user" title="Stephanie ">Stephanie </a>

        rated it

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/442087.My_Legendary_Girlfriend" title="Paperback 9780767906555" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/300958-stephanie?shelf=old-favorites" class="actionLinkLite">old-favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer633506679">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8122959266789722738">I fell head over heels in love with Mike Gayle's sophomore release MR. COMMITMENT, so when I stumbled across MY LEGENDARY GIRLFRIEND - which happens to be his first book, I had to read it! I was not disappointed!<br /><br />As usual Gayle takes his time when telling a story. There are many parts of the book that will have you screaming "hurry up!", but his well thought out characters and plot is what makes this book a hit.<br /><br />Will is the ill at ease, sarcastic protagonist in this delightful novel. It's been thr</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText8122959266789722738">I fell head over heels in love with Mike Gayle's sophomore release MR. COMMITMENT, so when I stumbled across MY LEGENDARY GIRLFRIEND - which happens to be his first book, I had to read it! I was not disappointed!<br /><br />As usual Gayle takes his time when telling a story. There are many parts of the book that will have you screaming "hurry up!", but his well thought out characters and plot is what makes this book a hit.<br /><br />Will is the ill at ease, sarcastic protagonist in this delightful novel. It's been three years and he still hasn't gotten over the day his ex-girlfriend Aggi dumped him - on his 23rd birthday - without rhyme or reason.<br /><br />There hasn't been a woman since who has come and knocked ol' Aggi down from that tremendously high pedestal Will has put her on. He obsesses over her day and night, and beats himself up trying to figure out what he could've done differently. He just cannot get her out of his system. That is until he gets a phone call from the girl who lived in his flat prior to him moving in. Could this stranger be the one who helps Will come to grips on the true meaning of love?<br /><br />In just one weekend, he learns what usually takes a lifetime for some. Maybe there is someone out there that can measure up to his "legendary girlfriend".<br /></span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="8122959266789722738">...more</a>

          </span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review nosyndicate" id="review_68984949">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/68984949" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/2670571-kaion" class="left imgcol" title="Kaion"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1443816759p2/2670571.jpg" alt="Kaion" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/68984949?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Aug 26, 2009</a>

      <a href="/user/show/2670571-kaion" class="user" title="Kaion">Kaion</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/442087.My_Legendary_Girlfriend" title="Paperback 9780767906555" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/2670571-kaion?shelf=humor" class="actionLinkLite">humor</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/2670571-kaion?shelf=contemporary" class="actionLinkLite">contemporary</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/2670571-kaion?shelf=essential" class="actionLinkLite">essential</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer68984949">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11491392131455731261"><strong>Summary:</strong> On the eve of his 26th birthday weekend, Will Kelly could be having a quarter-life crisis... He's been an English teacher for less than a month and he's bumming cigarettes off students. His best male friend is an insufferably self-absorbed rock frontman type who just scored a record deal. His best female friend is incredibly grown-up and sucessful and lives too far away. He's going to have to beg for another student-banking overdraft extension. He's avoiding a clingy one-night stand, an</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText11491392131455731261"><strong>Summary:</strong> On the eve of his 26th birthday weekend, Will Kelly could be having a quarter-life crisis... He's been an English teacher for less than a month and he's bumming cigarettes off students. His best male friend is an insufferably self-absorbed rock frontman type who just scored a record deal. His best female friend is incredibly grown-up and sucessful and lives too far away. He's going to have to beg for another student-banking overdraft extension. He's avoiding a clingy one-night stand, and his one-room London flat is a cesspool. And worst of all, it's three years on- and he's still hopelessly obsessed with his 'legendary' ex-girlfriend Aggi.<br /><br />Will thinks he's just going to lie in and be pathetic this birthday weekend, but instead events conspire that will make him re-evaluate his life, transform all his major relationships, fall in love - and maybe, just maybe, finally get over Aggi.<br /><br /><strong>Review</strong>: <em>My Legendary Girlfriend</em> is a remarkably dynamic story, for consisting entirely of phone conversations. This is where Mike Gayle really shines, with snappy and funny and revealing dialogue between the characters. Will Kelly may be unhappy and obsessive- but he knows it- and Gayle really plays up the humor of the desperate situation while also being true to the very Will's very modern existential concerns.<br /><br />What is he going to do with his life? His career? What really makes or breaks a friendship? What is love and what is simply selfish fancy? How much do we really want to be not lonely?<br /><br />I think these topics are very relatable and universal to anyone who has ever felt rather lost in life. And I really ended up rooting for Will and cheering him on when he finally navigates out of these murky waters: shaping up, re-orienting- and finally starts living his life rather than miring on auto-pilot. Rating: 5 stars (Reread 3/5/2010)</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="11491392131455731261">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/564271966?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Mar 28, 2013</a>

      <a href="/user/show/1437382-kathy" class="user" title="Kathy">Kathy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok">it was ok</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer564271966">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9229437510347140243">I have just discovered Lad-Lit. What!? This is a thing that exists? And it's not just John Green?<br /><br />This guy, the protagonist Will Kelly, falls in and out of love with three different girls over three days, OVER THE TELEPHONE. Ridiculous. Such a corny ending too. Jeez, how many romance comedies are there that quote Wuthering Heights? Regardless, the ending made me giggle and tear up, even though I was rooting for Kate the whole time.<br /><br />"Kate's voice sounded magical, as if it had the power to do whatev</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText9229437510347140243">I have just discovered Lad-Lit. What!? This is a thing that exists? And it's not just John Green?<br /><br />This guy, the protagonist Will Kelly, falls in and out of love with three different girls over three days, OVER THE TELEPHONE. Ridiculous. Such a corny ending too. Jeez, how many romance comedies are there that quote Wuthering Heights? Regardless, the ending made me giggle and tear up, even though I was rooting for Kate the whole time.<br /><br />"Kate's voice sounded magical, as if it had the power to do whatever she commanded, and right at this moment she had told it to provide me with comfort. I felt like I'd been rescued from the clutches of an evil dragon by a knightess in shining armour. If it had been possible for her to have lifted me up in her arms and carried me to safety, I honesty believe I couldn't have thought of anything I wanted more at this very moment."<br /><br />"I laughed inwardly. This was East of Eden, Pretty in Pink, St. Elmo's Fire and The Breakfast Club rolled into one. Be that as it may, I couldn't hold in what I had to say just because I was treading on the same hallowed ground as James Dean, Molly Ringwald, Emilio Estevez, Judd Nelson and thousands of other celluloid coming-of-agers trying to navigate their way through to adulthood. My life would resemble a teen movie until the day I died--I guarantee I'll be the only eighty-year-old man in the world suffering from teen angst."</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="9229437510347140243">...more</a>

              <a href="/review/list/5527647-rise?shelf=british-lit" class="actionLinkLite">british-lit</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer189308553">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15260254052738024517">Membaca Turning Thirty itu menyenangkan dan menghibur meskipun bukan novel yang luar biasa. Karena itu, aku pikir nggak ada salahnya mencoba baca buku My Legendary Girlfriend dengan asumsi bisa menghibur. Rupanya aku salah. My Legendary Girlfriend bercerita tentang William Kelly, yang akan berusia 26 tahun di awal cerita. Will baru seminggu menjadi guru SMP, tinggal di apartemen kumuh di London, dan masih terobsesi dengan mantan pacarnya yang telah putus tiga tahun lalu, Aggi. Seperti judulnya,</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText15260254052738024517">Membaca Turning Thirty itu menyenangkan dan menghibur meskipun bukan novel yang luar biasa. Karena itu, aku pikir nggak ada salahnya mencoba baca buku My Legendary Girlfriend dengan asumsi bisa menghibur. Rupanya aku salah. My Legendary Girlfriend bercerita tentang William Kelly, yang akan berusia 26 tahun di awal cerita. Will baru seminggu menjadi guru SMP, tinggal di apartemen kumuh di London, dan masih terobsesi dengan mantan pacarnya yang telah putus tiga tahun lalu, Aggi. Seperti judulnya, My Legendary Girlfriend ditujukan mengenai kenangan Will terhadap pacarnya yang legendaris yaitu Aggi. Di sepanjang novel, Will akan selalu mengingat BANYAK hal mengenai Aggi. Aggi begini, Aggi begitu, Aggi akan seperti ini dan itu. Sedangkan gambar telepon di sampulnya menunjukkan aktivitas Will yang bepusat di sekitar telepon di mana dia bisa merasa hidupnya lebih baik. Sungguh deh, bukannya terhibur membaca novel ini, aku malah merasa frutasi dan super sebal dengan Will yang kebanyakan waktunya dihabiskan dengan meratapi nasibnya dan Aggi. Yang lebih menyebalkan lagi dari novel ini adalah terjemahnnya nggak bagus yang membuat kalimat-kalimat yang ada menjadi aneh dan nggak logis. Dan sesungguhnya Tom adalah adik Will yang lebih muda delapan tahun, tapi di beberapa bagian di novel diterjemahkan sebagai "KAKAK". Sungguh menyebalkan. </span>

Grant Repka is an obscure indie rock musician who, in his forties, finds his career surprisingly resurrected with the success of his comic operetta about the doomed romance of Tommy Lee and Pamela Anderson. When Grant and Lisa meet after one of his shows, sparks don’t immediately fly—but e-mail addresses are exchanged. A my-book-for-your-CD trade and a couple of e-mails later, Lisa tells Grant that she enjoys his song “My Psycho Ex,” but warns him that where psycho-exes are concerned, she’s pretty sure she “could drink him under the table.”Little does she know that this will become the opening salvo in an epic e-mail battle dubbed the Psycho Ex Game, a storytelling competition in which horrific tales of dysfunctional love and living with lunatics are volleyed with glee. The rules are simple; the point system, unique: the experiences that would normally leave someone running for the therapist’s office (humiliation, degradation, and complicity in psychotic behavior) just might win match point in the Psycho Ex Game. Now it’s Grant vs. Lisa as the wretched tales of his ex, the Junkie Queen of Darkness, vie with the woe inflicted by her ex, a tantrum-throwing actor/director widely known as Mr. Summer Box Office Record-Holder.As the correspondence evolves, it surprises Lisa by offering her the kind of intimacy she has never shared with a man in the same room. Before long, what started as a friendly competition becomes a road map to an unlikely couple’s growing involvement, leaving both Grant and Lisa secretly wondering, “If we were to get involved, which one of us is potentially the next Psycho Ex?”Written in alternating he said/she said chapters, The Psycho Ex Game is shot through with the acerbic humor of Merrill Markoe and the mordant observations that have made Andy Prieboy a literate voice in rock.     <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/46977.Mike_Gayle">About Mike Gayle</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/46977.Mike_Gayle"><img alt="46977" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1266386567p2/46977.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer1653422789626591850">I was born in the 70s — the 70s were great. I would recommend them to anyone.<br /><br />I was also born in Birmingham — in my humble opinion the greatest city in the world with the nicest people too.<br /><br />I used to live in London — a great city too. But a bit on the pricey side.<br /><br />I also used to live in Manchester — another great city (although technically I lived in Salford which is next door but that’s sort of spli</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText1653422789626591850">I was born in the 70s — the 70s were great. I would recommend them to anyone.<br /><br />I was also born in Birmingham — in my humble opinion the greatest city in the world with the nicest people too.<br /><br />I used to live in London — a great city too. But a bit on the pricey side.<br /><br />I also used to live in Manchester — another great city (although technically I lived in Salford which is next door but that’s sort of splitting hairs).<br /><br />Before I went to university I wanted to be a social worker — I have no idea why. It didn’t last long.<br /><br />After I left university I wanted to write for the NME — I’ve always loved music but it was only when I went to uni that it started loving me back. I can’t play any instruments or sing so writing about music seemed to make sense.<br /><br />My first paid writing gig was for a listings magazine in Birmingham — (Actually my first unpaid writing gig was an interview with Kitchens of Distinction for Salford Student Magazine. I can’t begin to tell you how terrible it was.)<br /><br />I used to write a music fanzine — it was called Incredibly Inedible and I co-edited it with my mate Jackie. We typed up the first issue on my dad’s olde worlde typewriter and then literally cut and paste on to A4 sheets using scissors and glue. Over the three years of its existence we interviewed many bands and artists including: Smashing Pumpkins, The Cranberries, Pavement, Bill Hicks and Blur.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="1653422789626591850">...more</a>

    </div>
